Previously, if you used the Instant Replay button (shown below) on your Roku remote, you would see up to the last five channels you viewed since opening Sling.          To view your previous channels now, just hit the OK\u00a0button. This will bring up your player controls, and Last channel\u00a0will be highlighted. Miss a play in the game you were watching, or couldn't understand a line of dialogue? Hitting the Instant Replay\u00a0button will allow you to quick-rewind twenty seconds to see it again. If you'd like, you can also set up captions to display when you hit Instant Replay\u00a0from your Roku menu by selecting Settings, Captions,\u00a0then Instant Replay.\u00a0     Note: This feature is not available on all channels. Amazon Fire Tablet   To find out if an update is available for Sling TV on your Amazon tablet, visit the App Store on your device. \u00a0Let's start by returning to your home screen.  \u00a0       \u00a0  Then tap\u00a0Apps.          Tap\u00a0Store, located on the top\u00a0right\u00a0corner of your screen, to open the App Store.       \u00a0     Once the App store has launched, look to the top\u00a0left\u00a0corner of your screen to locate the\u00a0menu\u00a0icon. \u00a0Click on the\u00a0menu\u00a0icon.  \u00a0          Scroll down within your menu until you land on\u00a0App Updates. Tap\u00a0App Updates. \u00a0All of your apps in need of an update will be available here.         If an update is available for Sling TV, tap the\u00a0Update\u00a0button located beside the Sling TV app details.        Tap Update\u00a0to being installing the update   Once the installation process is complete click\u00a0Open, located where\u00a0Update\u00a0was previously. \u00a0Your Sling TV App will launch. Return to your stream and enjoy! \u00a0        Apple TV  Your Apple TV is set to automatically update your applications. If you turned this function off, return to the App Store and select Sling TV. If an update is available, select Update.  Android Device   Typically, your Android device will launch a pop-up window notifying you of an available update. \u00a0If you click\u00a0OK,\u00a0you will automatically be redirected to the Google Play Store. If you do not click\u00a0OK, you can still access the update. To do so, open the\u00a0Google Play Store.             Locate your Sling TV App by using the search engine.  \u00a0          If an update is available, you will see an\u00a0UPDATE button, as opposed to open. Click\u00a0UPDATE to begin the installation process.             Before the installation begins you must accept the Terms and Conditions. \u00a0Click\u00a0ACCEPT to continue with your update.             Allow the download and installation process to run its course.                  Once the update is complete, simply click\u00a0OPEN\u00a0to return to your stream!        Android TV   Typically, your Sling TV app will automatically update on your Android TV. If an update does not automatically occur, follow the steps below to check for and install any available updates. \u00a0  Return to your Android TV home screen, scroll\u00a0down\u00a0to\u00a0Apps, then find and launch the\u00a0Google Play Store.       \u00a0  Scroll\u00a0down\u00a0to\u00a0My Apps.       \u00a0  The top bar within\u00a0My Apps will display any available updates by app. Click on the Sling TV App if it is available under updates.   Now click\u00a0UPDATE.   Your Android TV will launch an App Permissions form. Press\u00a0Accept\u00a0to start the installation process.   Allow the download and installation process to run its course.   Once the update is complete, click\u00a0OPEN to launch your newly updated Sling TV app!          Google Chrome   Sling TV is supported on the most recent version of Google Chrome. Normally, Google Chrome updates automatically. If you still need to update your browser to watch Sling TV, open Google Chrome. \u00a0  In the top-right corner, click on the Settings icon.    Then click Update Google Chrome. If you do not see this option, this means you are on the latest version.  Finally, click relaunch.  To learn how to see what version of Google Chrome you are using, click here.   iOS Device   To check for, or install, an update temporarily leave the Sling TV app, then open your\u00a0App Store.             Look to the bottom right corner of your App Store to locate the\u00a0Updates\u00a0folder.             If an update is available for Sling TV it will be listed here. Simply click the\u00a0UPDATE\u00a0button, then allow the installation to run its course.           Roku   Typically your Sling TV app will automatically update on your Roku device. \u00a0If an update does not automatically occur follow the \u00a0steps below to check for and install any available updates.     Start by returning to your Roku home screen.          \u00a0Select Settings.  \u00a0\u00a0       Then System.          \u00a0Next, select System Update.             Click Check Now. \u00a0             Your Roku device will scan for any available updates across all applications.             If an updates is available, your Roku device will automatically install the update. \u00a0Once the update is complete click OK. \u00a0          Use the Home button on your remote to return to your home screen. Then, launch your Sling TV app and begin streaming.           Windows 10   Your Windows 10 device can automatically update applications the moment they become available. To enable automatic update, please follow the steps below.     To start, open the Windows Store.             Press, or click, the user icon near the search bar on the top-right corner of the page.             Press, or click, Settings from the drop down menu.             Under App updates\u00a0is Update apps automatically,\u00a0switch the toggle to the On\u00a0position.  *This should be the default setting on your Windows 10 device.             If you would prefer to check manually for app updates follow the steps below. \u00a0Open the Windows Store and click on the user icon. Now, press, or click, Downloads and updates.         Press, or click, the blue Check for updates\u00a0box, under the search bar.  *You can also check for updates for specific apps by visiting their page in the Windows Store. Normally, Google Chrome updates automatically. If you still need to update your browser to watch Sling TV, open Google Chrome. \u00a0</p><p dir=\"ltr\">In the top-right corner, click on the Settings icon.</p><p dir=\"ltr\"><a href=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/4YvyHMA-n1mNsA0uo31mUA2YLIwS-ljUWhJ3dcgT6qaQ5JeE8o4DM3wGE5hJ1bY3s0DEHcge18eZ7-uQTFXeea13kxmtdi8Uv9Ex4eKsz13ZgfKzkk9EG-PtIxJL2vjw7Veh66m7\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><img src=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/4YvyHMA-n1mNsA0uo31mUA2YLIwS-ljUWhJ3dcgT6qaQ5JeE8o4DM3wGE5hJ1bY3s0DEHcge18eZ7-uQTFXeea13kxmtdi8Uv9Ex4eKsz13ZgfKzkk9EG-PtIxJL2vjw7Veh66m7\" style=\"width: 624px; height: 341px;\" class=\"fr-dii\" alt=\"image of google home page on chrome browser with menu highlighted\"></a><br><br>Then click Update Google Chrome. If you do not see this option, this means you are on the latest version.</p><p dir=\"ltr\">Finally, click relaunch.</p><p dir=\"ltr\">To learn how to see what version of Google Chrome you are using, click <a href=\"/support/solutions/articles/33000219672-how-do-i-check-if-i-m-using-the-most-recent-version-of-google-chrome-\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">here</a>.</p></div><h4><strong>iOS Device</strong></h4><div><p>To check for, or install, an update temporarily leave the Sling TV app, then open your<span>\u00a0</span><em>App Store</em>.</p><p><br></p><p><img class=\"fr-dib fr-fil\" src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000548/original/ap_Wp2QhV-ZNNvF2bgOQtydy-DieWZHDTQ.png?1532024673\" data-filelink=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000548/original/ap_Wp2QhV-ZNNvF2bgOQtydy-DieWZHDTQ.png?1532024673\" data-fileid=\"46000000548\" data-uniquekey=\"1532023399954\" style=\"width: 498px; height: 374.504px;\" alt=\"image of iOS home screen with app store highlighted\"></p><p><br></p><p><br></p><p>Look to the bottom right corner of your App Store to locate the<span>\u00a0</span><em>Updates</em><span>\u00a0</span>folder.</p><p><br></p><p><br></p><p><img class=\"fr-dib fr-fil\" src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000549/original/-_f4pbVetknajKk5ihxcmTlbZRE8U9sUcA.png?1532024754\" style=\"width: 496px; height: 372px;\" data-filelink=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000549/original/-_f4pbVetknajKk5ihxcmTlbZRE8U9sUcA.png?1532024754\" data-fileid=\"46000000549\" data-uniquekey=\"1532023399954\" alt=\"image of app store with updates highlighted\"></p><p><br></p><p>If an update is available for Sling TV it will be listed here. If you don't see this experience, you can customize your favorite channels on the\u00a0My TV screen in the Sling app. Jump to Next Steps\u00a0below to learn more.     Once you've finished creating your account, select Personalize Your Experience\u00a0to select your favorite channels. Next Steps      Click WATCH NOW to start watching right away on your Google Chrome\u00a0browser or to download Google Chrome.         Prefer to watch on another device? Scroll down the page and select See all devices\u00a0to see all the different devices that support Sling, and get help installing the app on your device. Find more help here.    Once you've installed the Sling app and signed in to your account, personalize your experience by adding your favorite channels and shows to the My TV\u00a0screen. Learn more here.            ADDITIONAL SIGNUP OPTIONS:     You can also sign up directly through the Sling app on select devices.\u00a0If you don't have a device, or you'd like to take advantage of one of our prepaid offers to receive a free or discounted devices, choose Device Bundle\u00a0below for details.     Choose an option below to learn more       ANDROID TV, ANDROID DEVICE, LG TV, WINDOWS 10, XBOX ONE    Now that you have finished downloading our app to your device, it\u2019s time to sign up! To get started, select the sign up button on the Sling app's landing page.    The first page details your base service options. You can select Sling Orange, Sling Blue, or both (Sling Orange + Sling Blue).     Press\u00a0CONTINUE\u00a0to learn about our extra services. \u00a0Highlight over each service to learn more about the channels they include. \u00a0Click\u00a0Add\u00a0to add an extra to your subscription. If you change your mind, click on the green checkmark to deselect.     Now it is time to create your account. \u00a0Start with your email address, then create a unique and secure password.          Next enter your billing information. Your subscription total, by service, will be described on the right side of your screen. Be sure to review your subscription before pressing\u00a0FINISH & SUBMIT.          Lastly, press\u00a0FINISH & SUBMIT.\u00a0Now that your subscription has been processed it is time to start streaming! Enjoy!        ROKU   We are very excited for you to join us! Click on the Sling TV thumbnail on your Roku device to get started, then select the signup button.     Roku and Sling have teamed up to make signing up quick and easy for you. \u00a0Your Sling TV account will be created through your registered Roku account. Confirm the email address, zip code, and name registered with your Roku are correct.          Next, create your Sling TV account by adding a unique and secure password.          Now it is time to create your subscription! The first page details your base service options. You can select Sling Orange, Sling Blue, or both (Sling Orange + Sling Blue). Next, check out the available extras to learn more about the included channels. Click Add, to select your service and any available extras.     Once you have selected your service just press Finish & Submit. \u00a0Your subscription will be charged to your Roku account after completion of your free trial.          Your new Sling TV account will launch automatically. \u00a0Enjoy!      AMAZON FIRE     Once you've downloaded the Sling TV app, it is time to create your account. Launch the Sling TV app, then select the signup button  The first page details your base service options. You can select Sling Orange, Sling Blue, or both (Sling Orange + Sling Blue), or select View More Languages\u00a0to see all of our in-language programming options. Once you have determined the best base services for you, select Add,\u00a0then select Continue.  Next, check out our available extra services. Some examples include Cloud DVR service, Kids, Lifestyle or Sports. Select the Add\u00a0button to add an extra service. To deselect a service, select the green check mark. Once your service is customized just the way you'd like, select Continue.\u00a0   Now it's time to create your account. Enter your email address, then create a unique and secure password.    Review your subscription total. Select Finish & Submit.    To provide you with great local and regional channels (where available), Sling TV requests your ZIP code. This screen is Amazon asking for your approval to send us your ZIP code. Select I agree\u00a0to continue.    You can also create your Parental Controls login. To do so, select Enable.    Now click subscribe to activate your Sling TV service. If you have selected any extra services, you will repeat this step for each service.    To finalize your subscription with Sling TV, Amazon will request your Amazon password to authenticate the transaction.    Your Sling TV subscription is complete! Select Close\u00a0and enjoy your new service!        XFINITY\u00a0   Please note that Sling Orange, Sling Blue, Sling Orange + Sling Blue, and select Latino services are not\u00a0available on the Xfinity platform.     Already a Sling TV customer? Next, create your account by entering your email address and creating a unique and secure password. To see all available device offers, visit sling.com/devices/offers. Please note that device bundle offers are not currently available to Sling TV customers in Puerto Rico.\u00a0  If you know the device offer you'd like to sign up for, click on GET THIS OFFER,\u00a0or click on OFFER DETAILS\u00a0to compare other offers. Please note that if your Sling TV subscription is billed through a third party, you will not be able to register for a device bundle at this time.    Once you've selected your offer by clicking GET THIS OFFER,\u00a0create your account using your email address and a unique and secure password that you've created.  Once you've finished selecting your services, enter your billing and shipping information.   On the right side of your screen, choose your shipping method, and review your subscription total along with the discounted price of your new device. After review, click FINISH & SUBMIT.    Your account creation is complete! If you don\u2019t already see the Sling TV app on your Home screen, you\u2019ll need to download it. Follow the steps below to download the Sling TV app on your<span>\u00a0</span><a href=\"http://help.sling.com/en/support/solutions/articles/33000219125-what-models-of-lg-tv-can-i-use-for-sling-tv-\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">supported</a> LG Smart TV.</p><p><br></p><p>Start by returning to your LG home screen by pressing the<span>\u00a0</span><em>Home</em><span>\u00a0</span>button on your remote. Then select<span>\u00a0</span><em>Search</em>.</p><p><br></p><p>Enter \u201cSling\u201d using the on-screen keyboard and select<span>\u00a0</span><em>Search</em>.</p><p><br></p><p>Highlight and select the Sling TV app.</p><p><br></p><p>Select<span>\u00a0</span><em>Install</em>.</p><p><br></p><p>Allow the download and installation process to complete.</p><p><br></p><p>Once the download is complete, click<span>\u00a0</span><em>Launch</em><span>\u00a0</span>to open the Sling TV app! Constant speed of 3.0 Megabits per second (Mb/s) or more - Streaming video content on portable devices such as tablets or phones  Constant speed of 5.0 Mb/s or more - Single stream of video content on a TV, PC, or Mac  Constant speed of 25 Mb/s or more - Recommended for households that maintain internet usage on multiple devices       If your internet service provider (ISP) has a cap on your data, it's a good idea to keep an eye on your usage while streaming.\u00a0     Find out to check bandwidth usage below. On your <span class=\"match\">Roku</span> or Android","type":"ARTICLE","url":"/en/support/solutions/articles/46000000383-what-is-sling-free-","source":{"article":{"art_type":null,"created_at":"2019-09-17T12:05:14-06:00","desc_un_html":"   Sling Free is a way for you to check out Sling and what we have to offer with no commitments.     Watch as much free content as you'd like, and come back at any time as often as you'd like to browse free shows and movies from many of the same channels you'll find with a Sling subscription.     Choose an option below for more information:      Am I being billed for Sling Free?      Nope! Just like the name says,\u00a0Sling Free\u00a0is totally free to you.     As a Sling Free user, you will have the option to rent movies or purchase Pay-Per-View events. For these, you will need to create an account by adding an email address and password along with billing information. However, if you don't start a Sling subscription, you won't be billed outside of these one-time purchases.     Note: If you've added billing information for Pay-Per-View purchases or movie rentals, you can restrict future purchases by enabling parental controls.\u00a0Learn more about parental controls.      How do I get Sling Free?      Sling Free is available on Roku and Android TV devices as well as select web browsers. On your Roku or Android TV device, you'll need to\u00a0install the Sling app. Once you've installed and launched the Sling app, select Browse as Guest to start watching.\u00a0     On your web browser, you can head to \u00a0watch.sling.com to start watching.     We're hoping to have this experience available on additional devices in the coming months.      What will I see on Sling Free?      When you first launch Sling Free, you'll be placed on to our My TV page. Here, you can view our top free content, as well as see what Sling subscribers are currently watching.\u00a0     Under the Guide tab, you can view content available from each channel in Sling Free. If a channel has free live programming available, you'll see this in the guide. If the channel says See all available content, select this to view available Video On-Demand titles. If you'd still like to cancel, click Continue to Cancel,\u00a0then Confirm My Cancellation.          Your account has now been cancelled. We'll let you know when the cancellation will take effect, and where we'll send confirmation.           After you cancel, \u00a0your current paid subscription will run for the duration of your billing cycle or for any prepaid period. This means you can enjoy your subscription until your renewal date. If you cancel during a free trial, service will be terminated immediately. Please note that we do not provide refunds for prepaid or partial months of service.  For more information about our cancellation policy, see our Terms of Use.      See below for additional questions:     When will my cancellation take effect?      If you're currently in a free trial, your service will be cancelled immediately.\u00a0     For paid subscribers, your cancellation will take effect at the end of your current billing cycle. This also applies to prepaid periods.\u00a0     See below for examples.   Monthly:\u00a0If you're billed on the 15th of each month, and cancel your subscription on the 12th, you'll continue to have service until the 15th.  Prepaid:\u00a0If you signed up for a three-month prepaid offer\u00a0and cancel after a month, you'll continue to have service for the two months remaining in your offer period.  You can confirm your billing date by logging in to your account here\u00a0and checking under Your Subscription.\u00a0      Can I pause my Sling TV subscription?\u00a0   You bet!\u00a0  If you're moving, traveling, or just need a break from Sling for a bit, you can now pause your subscription.  To do so, sign in to your account at sling.com/account\u00a0and select Cancel Subscription.\u00a0You'll be presented with the option to pause. Select Pause My Subscription.       Next, select how long you'd like to pause your subscription for: One, two, or three months.  Important Note:\u00a0Your DVR recordings will be lost if you select to Pause for longer than one month.  Once you've selected how long you'd like to pause your subscription for, select Next.       Finally, review the details on your Pause, including the date it will take effect, the date your subscription will restart, and what you'll be subscribed to when it restarts. Select Confirm Pause\u00a0to finalize.       The Pause will take effect at the end\u00a0of your current billing cycle and will automatically restart on the date shown.\u00a0  If you'd like to restart your service before the automatic restart, log in to your account at sling.com/account\u00a0and select Restart Now.    Important note:\u00a0Customers currently taking advantage of a promotion (prepay device bundle, annual plan or free trial), customers using only a Sling TV gift card as a payment method, customers that signed up through their device (excluding Roku), customers that signed up through an affiliate retail partner or customers that are using Amazon Pay are ineligible to pause their accounts at this time. If you recently cancelled your Sling TV subscription, you\u2019ll continue to have service until the end of your current billing cycle. If you cancelled during a free trial, your service will have been terminated immediately.\u00a0Once your account expires following the end of your last billing cycle, you can still access hours of free content from Sling TV whether you have an active subscription or not.  Please note that while the full experience described below will only be available on Roku devices to start, many features are available on other devices, and we hope to have the full experience available on all devices in the coming months.  To start, launch your Sling TV app. From here, select Restart Service\u00a0to restart your subscription just the way you had it before, Change Subscription\u00a0to restart your subscription with a new service, or Browse Free Shows\u00a0to check out some free programming.    If you\u2019d just like to check out some free shows, choose from channels like TBS, TruTV, TNT, Food Network, HGTV, and History Channel. How many devices can I watch free content on? You can enjoy free content from Sling TV on two devices at one time with your expired account. If you restart your subscription, you'll be able to stream on the number of devices included with that service. Can I rent movies or Pay-Per-View? For an additional cost, you can watch CBS programming - including NFL Football in your area - with the CBS All Access app. CBS All Access is available on many of the same devices you use to watch Sling TV, including Roku, Amazon Fire and Apple TV.     In select cities, you can also watch local programming from CBS and FOX for free using the Locast app, available at locast.org,\u00a0or downloading the app on your Android or iOS smartphone/tablet, Amazon Fire device or Roku.     An HD antenna will also allow you to watch your local programming over the air for free. for free in select cities using the Locast app, available at <strong>locast.org,\u00a0</strong>or downloading the app on your Android or iOS smartphone/tablet, Amazon Fire device or Sling does not own the networks provided on our service \u2013 we have to pay programmers for the right to offer their channels to our customers. Unfortunately, programming prices have risen, and they continue to climb with no end in sight, despite our focus on negotiating fair deals. Sling is absorbing some of the cost, instead of passing everything on to you.     While there are other options out there, Sling TV remains the best value for live sports and news, and Sling is the only service that gives cord cutters the ability to customize their TV experience at an unbeatable value.     For additional answers, choose an option below:      How do I know if my price is changing?      We\u2019re communicating with all customers via email beginning December 23rd, 2019.      How much is my price changing?      For Sling base services, you will see the following changes:   Sling Orange\u00a0is now $30/month  Sling Blue\u00a0is now $30/month  Sling Orange + Sling Blue\u00a0is now $45/month   The 4 Extras Deal\u00a0is now $12/month for Sling Orange, Sling Blue and Sling Orange + Sling Blue subscribers.     Sports Extras\u00a0is now $15/month for Sling Orange + Sling Blue\u00a0subscribers. Sports Extra remains $10 per month as an add-on to either Sling Orange or Sling Blue.     The Total TV Deal\u00a0is now $25/month for Sling Orange + Sling Blue\u00a0subscribers. Total TV Deal remains $20 per month as an add-on to either Sling Orange or Sling Blue.     Any other extras you subscribe to, including Cloud DVR Plus, will remain unaffected.      When will my price change?      New Sling subscribers will see the updated price beginning December 23, 2019.     Existing subscribers will see the price change on their next bill after January 22, 2020.     Important Note:\u00a0If making changes to your subscription prior to January 22, 2020, you will be billed for the new prices listed above.     For subscribers with an account currently on pause, new pricing will take affect once the account is un-paused.     If you need to confirm your billing date, log in to your account at sling.com/account and check your auto-renew date, or get more information by selecting View Billing Details.      Am I getting more channels?      Since we launched in 2015, we have not raised the price of Sling Blue, although we have added 17 channels, the most recent being with the introduction of FOX News, MSNBC and HLN to the Sling Blue base service.\u00a0     We\u2019ve also added four networks to Sling Orange since the last price increase, in June 2018, and have grown one of the largest on-demand libraries with more than 126,000 titles across all Sling services, up from 12,000 titles at the end of 2015.\u00a0  Some of the latest features we\u2019ve launched include Cloud DVR Free, which includes 10 hours of Cloud DVR, plus the ability to record all Disney and ESPN channels, full player controls (like fast-forward and pause) across all recordable channels, a new ribbons to help with content discovery, like Trending Live and Recommended for You, as well as improved search and a binge-watching feature.     We continue to revamp the experiences across our platforms, including a refreshed UI on Apple TV and Roku devices, new guide on Roku devices, new search and micro guide on LG, Samsung and Xbox One devices, and \u2018launch into live\u2019 and \u2018browse while watching\u2019 features on Apple TV.     In the last half of 2019, Sling launched on Safari desktop, Android Chrome mobile, Facebook Portal and Google Nest Hub / Nest Hub Max \u2013 giving customers access to their favorite content on over 20 platforms.      Will this keep happening?      While we do everything in our power to fight for customers and keep prices low, we can\u2019t say if your price will change in the future. Programming prices continue to rise we no end in sight, but we work hard to negotiate fair deals that keep your prices as low as possible.         ","description":"<div id=\"pkb-accordion\"><div><p>We work hard for fair deals that keep your channel costs as low as possible. Sling does not own the networks provided on our service \u2013 we have to pay programmers for the right to offer their channels to our customers. Unfortunately, programming prices have risen, and they continue to climb with no end in sight, despite our focus on negotiating fair deals. Sling is absorbing some of the cost, instead of passing everything on to you.</p><p><br></p><p>While there are other options out there, Sling TV remains the best value for live sports and news, and Sling is the only service that gives cord cutters the ability to customize their TV experience at an unbeatable value.</p><p><br></p><p><em>For additional answers, choose an option below:</em></p><p><br></p></div><h4><strong>How do I know if my price is changing?</strong></h4><div><p><br></p><p>We\u2019re communicating with all customers via email beginning <strong>December 23<sup>rd</sup>, 2019.</strong></p><p><br></p></div><h4><strong>How much is my price changing?</strong></h4><div><p><br></p><p>For Sling base services, you will see the following changes:</p><ul><li><strong>Sling Orange\u00a0</strong>is now $30/month</li><li><strong>Sling Blue\u00a0</strong>is now $30/month</li><li><strong>Sling Orange + Sling Blue\u00a0</strong>is now $45/month</li></ul><p>The <strong>4 Extras Deal\u00a0</strong>is now $12/month for <strong>Sling Orange</strong>, <strong>Sling Blue</strong> and <strong>Sling Orange + Sling Blue</strong> subscribers.</p><p><br></p><p><strong>Sports Extras\u00a0</strong>is now $15/month for <strong>Sling Orange + Sling Blue\u00a0</strong>subscribers. Sports Extra remains $10 per month as an add-on to either Sling Orange or Sling Blue.</p><p><br></p><p>The <strong>Total TV Deal\u00a0</strong>is now $25/month for <strong>Sling Orange + Sling Blue\u00a0</strong>subscribers. Total TV Deal remains $20 per month as an add-on to either Sling Orange or Sling Blue.</p><p><br></p><p><em>Any other extras you subscribe to, including Cloud DVR Plus, will remain unaffected.</em></p><p><br></p></div><h4><strong>When will my price change?</strong></h4><div><p><br></p><p>New Sling subscribers will see the updated price beginning <strong>December 23, 2019</strong>.</p><p><br></p><p>Existing subscribers will see the price change on their next bill after <strong>January 22, 2020</strong>.</p><p><br></p><p><strong><em>Important Note:\u00a0</em></strong><em>If making changes to your subscription prior to January 22, 2020, you will be billed for the new prices listed above.</em></p><p><br></p><p>For subscribers with an account currently on pause, new pricing will take affect once the account is un-paused.</p><p><br></p><p>If you need to confirm your billing date, log in to your account at sling.com/account and check your auto-renew date, or get more information by selecting <a href=\"https://www.sling.com/account/billing_information\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" target=\"_blank\"><em><strong>View Billing Details</strong></em></a><em>.</em></p><p><br></p></div><h4><strong>Am I getting more channels?</strong></h4><div><p><br></p><p>Since we launched in 2015, we have not raised the price of Sling Blue, although we have added 17 channels, the most recent being with the introduction of <strong>FOX News</strong>, <strong>MSNBC</strong> and <strong>HLN</strong> to the Sling Blue base service.\u00a0</p><p><br></p><p>We\u2019ve also added four networks to Sling Orange since the last price increase, in June 2018, and have grown one of the largest on-demand libraries with more than 126,000 titles across all Sling services, up from 12,000 titles at the end of 2015.\u00a0</p><p>Some of the latest features we\u2019ve launched include <strong>Cloud DVR Free</strong>, which includes Live</strong></a> and <a href=\"https://whatson.sling.com/announcements/sling-tv-gets-personal-on-apple-tv/\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" target=\"_blank\"><strong>Recommended for You</strong></a><u>,</u> as well as improved search and a <a href=\"https://whatson.sling.com/announcements/sling-tv-launches-free-experience-for-all/\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" target=\"_blank\"><strong>binge-watching feature</strong></a>.</p><p><br></p><p>We continue to revamp the experiences across our platforms, including a <a href=\"https://whatson.sling.com/announcements/sling-refreshes-ui-on-apple-tv-and-roku/\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" target=\"_blank\"><strong>refreshed UI on Apple TV and Roku devices</strong></a>, Choose an option below to see more:     Why should I use an HD antenna?      Did you know that by 2020, local channels like CBS, ABC and FOX could cost you over $300/year? Unlike the other guys, Sling won't make you pay for local channels. It's just one of the many ways Sling helps you keep your monthly bill low, by offering a smarter solution to get you the live TV you love.     Modern HD antennas are compact, convenient and extremely affordable, plus setting one up is easy! Just position your antenna on or near a window, connect it to your TV and let it scan for channels in your area.\u00a0     Learn More      I'm too far away for an indoor antenna, what now?      We're happy to help find the best solution for you! Visit us here\u00a0to learn more.      Why aren't locals available in my city?      The local channels offered on Sling TV are limited to those owned and operated by their respective networks.      What is a DMA?      A Designated Market Area or DMA is a region usually centered around a large city that determines the programming you'll receive. Markets are usually named for the largest city or cities in the market.\u00a0     For Example:\u00a0The New York DMA includes not only New York City itself, but areas where New York channels are viewed the most. This includes areas surrounding the city, as well as party of New Jersey, Connecticut and Pennsylvania.     The DMA you are in determines what local and regional content you can receive.      How do Regional Sports Networks work?      Regional Sports Networks (RSNs) you can receive with your Sling Blue subscription are based on your billing ZIP code. Note that you can only\u00a0receive RSNs through your Sling TV subscription, and you won't be able to receive these channels over the air with an antenna. Click/tap images to see a larger version.</p><p><strong><br></strong></p><p><em><strong>What the local channels search tool looks like:</strong></em></p><p><br></p><p><em><img src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000020796/original/s1Afc8l568bOPbXN8mGB-uGp9-ZMpeG56g.png?1563312881\" class=\"fr-fic fr-dib fr-fil\" data-filelink=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000020796/original/s1Afc8l568bOPbXN8mGB-uGp9-ZMpeG56g.png?1563312881\" data-fileid=\"46000020796\" data-uniquekey=\"1563311983792\" style=\"width: 525px;\"></em></p><p>Enter your address and ZIP code, then select <em>See Available Channels</em></p><p><strong><br></strong></p><p><em><strong>How results may appear (local channel availability may vary based on your location):</strong></em></p><p><br></p><p><img src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000020803/original/tT5qjgEpcdXpeX4EGzdigVCaAVfA9z5d2Q.png?1563315615\" class=\"fr-fic fr-dib fr-fil\" data-filelink=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000020803/original/tT5qjgEpcdXpeX4EGzdigVCaAVfA9z5d2Q.png?1563315615\" data-fileid=\"46000020803\" data-uniquekey=\"1563311983792\" style=\"width: 674px;\"></p><p>Customer has no local channels available with Sling, but all major networks available with an indoor antenna.</p><p><br></p><p><img src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000020807/original/_7sAOZuboJimudY0A9e_89Rsq9E6NAzvCQ.png?1563316719\" class=\"fr-fic fr-dib fr-fil\" data-filelink=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000020807/original/_7sAOZuboJimudY0A9e_89Rsq9E6NAzvCQ.png?1563316719\" data-fileid=\"46000020807\" data-uniquekey=\"1563311983792\" style=\"width: 672px;\"></p><p>Customer has no local channels available with Sling; major networks are available with an outdoor antenna.</p><p><br></p></div><h4><strong>Are any other local channels available?</strong></h4><div><p><br></p><p>Additional local channels are not available at this time.</p><p><br></p><p>However, sporting events on ABC, such as college football and NBA basketball can be viewed on <strong>ESPN3,\u00a0</strong>available with your Sling Orange subscription.</p><p><br></p></div><h4><strong>Where will local channels be in my guide?</strong></h4><div><p><br></p><p>NBC and FOX will show up at the front of your guide when you subscribe to Sling Blue or Sling Orange + Sling Blue.</p><p><br></p><p><strong><em>Important Note:\u00a0</em></strong>If you're unable to receive <strong>live\u00a0</strong>local programming through your Sling subscription, NBC will be available as an On-Demand-only channel.</p><p><span style=\"font-size: 18px;\"><br></span></p></div><p><span style=\"font-size: 18px;\"><br></span></p><strong><span style=\"font-size: 18px;\">I can't get locals through Sling, how can I still watch?</span></strong><br><span style=\"font-size: 13px;\"><em>We still have options to make sure you can watch your favorite live local programming. Keep reading:\u00a0</em></span><p><br></p><h4><strong>Locast</strong></h4><div><p><br></p><p>In select cities<strong>,\u00a0</strong>you can watch your local channels for free using the Locast app or by visiting. <strong>locast.org.\u00a0</strong>The Locast app is available for your Android or iOS smartphone or tablet, laptop, Amazon Fire device or Roku device. Visit Locast to see a list of available cities.</p><p><br></p></div><h4><strong>CBS All Access</strong></h4><div><p><br></p><p>For an additional cost, you can download and watch CBS programming - including NFL Football - with the CBS All Access app. CBS All Access is available on many of the same devices you use to watch Sling TV, including Roku, Amazon Fire and Apple TV.</p><p><br></p></div><h4><strong>HD Antenna</strong></h4><div><p><br></p><p><span class=\"fr-video fr-dvi fr-draggable\"><iframe src=\"https://player.vimeo.com/video/330867935\" width=\"640\" height=\"360\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" class=\"fr-draggable\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts allow-forms allow-same-origin allow-presentation\"></iframe></span></p><p><br></p><p>Watch your favorites live, like your local news, sports such as NFL Football and hit shows - all for FREE - when you pair an HD antenna with your Sling subscription. Get FOX or NBC if they aren't available on Sling TV in your area, and watch channels like CBS, ABC, the CW and other local channels not on Sling. Hit the button below to see what channels you can see in your area and learn how to get an HD antenna on us:</p><p><br></p><p><a class=\"btn btn-theme-primary\" href=\"https://www.sling.com/programming/locals\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><strong>Get my antenna</strong></a></p><p><br></p><strong><em>Note:\u00a0</em></strong><em>Local broadcast channel availability varies based on geography.</em>\u00a0<p><br></p></div><p><br></p><p><strong><span style=\"font-size: 18px;\">Have more questions?</span></strong></p><p><em>Choose an option below to see more:</em></p><p><br></p><h4><strong>Why should I use an HD antenna?</strong></h4><div><p><br></p><p>Did you know that by 2020, local channels like CBS, ABC and FOX could cost you over $300/year? Unlike the other guys, Sling won't make you pay for local channels. It's just one of the many ways Sling helps you keep your monthly bill low, by offering a smarter solution to get you the live TV you love.</p><p><br></p><p>Modern HD antennas are compact, convenient and extremely affordable, plus setting one up is easy! Just position your antenna on or near a window, connect it to your TV and let it scan for channels in your area.\u00a0</p><p><br></p><p><a class=\"btn btn-theme-primary\" href=\"https://sling.com/programming/locals\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><strong>Learn More</strong></a></p><p><br></p></div><h4><strong>I'm too far away for an indoor antenna, what now?</strong></h4><div><p><br></p><p>We're happy to help find the best solution for you! Visit us <a href=\"https://www.airtv.net/antenna-installation/\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" target=\"_blank\"><strong>here</strong></a><strong>\u00a0</strong>to learn more.</p><p><br></p></div><h4><strong>Why aren't locals available in my city?</strong></h4><div><p><br></p><p>The local channels offered on Sling TV are limited to those owned and operated by their respective networks.</p><p><br></p></div><h4><strong>What is a DMA?</strong></h4><div><p><br></p><p>A Designated Market Area or DMA is a region usually centered around a large city that determines the programming you'll receive. Markets are usually named for the largest city or cities in the market.\u00a0</p><p><br></p><p><strong><em>For Example:\u00a0</em></strong>The New York DMA includes not only New York City itself, but areas where New York channels are viewed the most. This includes areas surrounding the city, as well as party of New Jersey, Connecticut and Pennsylvania.</p><p><br></p><p>The DMA you are in determines what local and regional content you can receive.</p><p><br></p></div><h4><strong>How do Regional Sports Networks work?</strong></h4><div><p><br></p><p>Regional Sports Networks (RSNs) you can receive with your Sling Blue subscription are based on your billing ZIP code. Note that you can <strong>only\u00a0</strong>receive RSNs through your Sling TV subscription, and you won't be able to receive these channels over the air with an antenna.
